<analysis>**original_problem_statement**: The user initiated the session reporting a critical issue where new user KYC (Know Your Customer) submissions were bypassing the admin review queue and remaining in a DRAFT state, preventing user onboarding.

Throughout the session, the user added numerous follow-up requests:
- **UI/UX Fixes**:
  - Resolve an issue on small mobile devices where header icons overlap with each other and with the iOS status bar (in PWA mode).
  - Fix a language toggle bug that incorrectly displayed IT IT instead of just IT.
- **Feature Requests**:
  - Display the client's name in the admin support ticket list for easier identification.
  - Create a Contact Support option that is always accessible to users, not just when their account is on tax hold.
  - Implement a password confirmation modal before a user can send money, as a security measure.
  - Add a feature for admins to clear all notifications for a specific user from the admin panel.
- **Bug Fixes**:
  - Fix a critical bug where entering an incorrect password in the new transfer confirmation modal logged the user out of the application.
- **Data Investigation & Restoration**:
  - Conduct a deep investigation into the transaction history of user Arben Hallulli.
  - Manually restore a transfer for Arben Hallulli that had been deleted, ensuring it reappeared in the admin approval queue.
- **General**:
  - The user repeatedly emphasized that this is a professional banking application with real clients, demanding extreme care, thorough testing with new test users only, and confirmation of 100% readiness before every deployment.

**User's preferred language**: English

**what currently exists?**
The application is a professional banking platform with a FastAPI backend and a React frontend. The following features and fixes were completed in this session:
- **KYC Workflow**: A + Queue User button was added for admins to manually push a user's KYC application into the review queue. The root cause (user not completing the form) was identified and backend validation was hardened. The specific user's stuck KYC was manually resolved.
- **Password-Protected Transfers**: A password confirmation modal now appears before a user can initiate a transfer. This is handled by a new, secure backend endpoint.
- **Critical Logout Bug**: A bug causing users to be logged out after entering an incorrect password during transfer confirmation has been fixed by making the global error handler more specific.
- **Admin Features**:
    - The admin support ticket list now displays the client's name and email.
    - Admins can now clear all notifications for a specific user via a new button in the user details panel.
- **Data Restoration**: A deleted €2,000 transfer for user Arben Hallulli was successfully investigated and restored to the admin Transfers Queue.
- **UI/UX Improvements**:
    - A Need Help? floating action button provides a persistent Contact Support option on the user dashboard.
    - The mobile header layout was fixed to prevent icons from overlapping on small screens.
    - PWA (Progressive Web App) display on iOS was fixed to respect the status bar safe area, preventing content overlap.
    - The language toggle display bug (IT IT) was resolved by removing unreliable flag emojis in favor of plain text.

**Last working item**:
- **Last item agent was working**: The agent implemented an admin feature to clear a user's notifications. Following this, the user requested a final confirmation that the application was 100% ready for redeployment. The agent ran a final comprehensive health check and test suite.

The system should be refactored to either use the ledger as the single source of truth for balance calculation or implement a robust sync/recalculation mechanism upon deletion/rejection.

    - **(P1) Scheduled/Recurring Transfers**: Allow users to set up automatic future-dated or recurring payments.

**Code Architecture**


**Key Technical Concepts**
- **PWA Safe Area Insets**: Used CSS  to adapt the UI for iOS devices in standalone (home screen app) mode, preventing the header from overlapping with the system status bar.
- **Targeted Axios Interceptor Logic**: Patched the global error handler in  to specifically ignore 401 errors from , preventing an incorrect global logout action while maintaining security for other session-expiry events.
- **MongoDB ObjectId vs. String Handling**: Resolved bugs by modifying database queries to correctly handle  fields that could be either a BSON  or a string, ensuring user lookups were successful.
- **Manual Data Restoration**: Performed a careful, multi-step investigation and manual insertion into the MongoDB  collection to restore a deleted record, ensuring it correctly linked to existing ledger entries.

**key DB schema**
- No schema changes were made. Work involved adding, modifying, and querying documents in the following collections: , , , , , , and .

**changes in tech stack**
- None.

**Areas that need refactoring**:
- The balance calculation logic is brittle. The discrepancy found during the investigation (database balance showing €0 while ledger entries summed to €8,000) indicates that the  field is not reliably synced. The balance should ideally be calculated dynamically from the  or have a more robust recalculation trigger.

**key api endpoints**
- **NEW**:  - Allows an admin to manually force a user's KYC application into the 'SUBMITTED' queue for review.
- **NEW**:  - A secure endpoint for the currently authenticated user to verify their own password. Returns success or a 401 error.
- **NEW**:  - Allows an admin to delete all notifications for a given user.
- **MODIFIED**:  - Now includes  and  in the response for each ticket.

**Critical Info for New Agent**
- **User's Core Requirement: Stability.** The user manages a live banking application with real clients. Stability and avoiding regressions are the absolute highest priorities. Every change must be tested thoroughly, preferably with new test users created by the testing agent.
- **Data Integrity Risk**: A significant finding was that a user's account balance () can go out of sync if related transactions in the  collection are deleted. The  seem to remain correct. This is a potential source of major bugs and should be addressed proactively.
- **PWA/Mobile Testing**: UI bugs related to PWA mode (like the safe area fix) are difficult to verify with automated screenshots alone. The user may need to test on a real device to confirm the fix.
